My stairway to heaven: First,I have quartz stairs  Second  Level 1: Avoid the magma!  All you need: â€¢ Magma blocks  â€¢ Lime concrete  â€¢ Zombie spawn egg(64) â€¢ Iron bars  â€¢ Cell door  â€¢ Redstone dust  â€¢ Redstone torch  â€¢ Lever  â€¢ Iron door  Build a maze with the lime concrete  Then,Creat 2 cells  After that add 32 zombies in one of the cells  That way if the others die,the rest will keep going  Now,back to the main topic  The maze needs to be complicated If it's to easy,you may run away from the zombies too quickly! That's why,Make a complicated maze where you will have to choose between 3 options  If your favorite side is middle,then make the middle one the wrong one  If your favorite side is left,then make the left one the wrong one  If your favorite side is right,then make the right one the wrong one  All you need: â€¢ A Magma block  All you just need is a Magma block! If your favorite side is right,then put a Magma block in front of the right one  Then,on the left side,break the quartz blocks below you  That way the middle one is correct  Same will happen twice  Level 2: Magma parkour  This time it's a bit different  All you need: â€¢ Magma blocks  â€¢ Quartz blocks  If you make it too easy,you will pass on! So make the quartz platforms distanced from each other  That way,If you try to jump to the second platform,you're doomed by the Magma blocks  The last platform will be the biggest,but make sure you don't make it too close! If you make it close,you will jump to easily to the last platform  So,make it 10x10  Last level,You have to beat the final boss,an ENDERMAN! And not any ordinary Enderman,This Enderman has 300 health  Now,before you settle the final Boss room,set a chest full of diamond armour  Then,pass on to the final boss room  If you want to escape from the Enderman,then you will add a special ability to the Enderman  WARPING!  Like other Endermen,this Enderman can warp  You will have no way to escape  The only way to escape is to kill the boss  Once you kill the boss,you meet in heaven
